</font><font color="#804040">north
</font><font color="#808000">Centre of the Necropolis.
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">Rubescent lambency emits from amidst crimson petals of the weeping amaranth 
suspended from a magnificent gemwork chandelier.</font><font color="#008080"> Rising up from cracks in the 
floor, the Megalith of Doom towers above everything here, polluting the air with
its foul fumes. The Keeper of the Megalith stands here radiating a tainted 
presence. A painting of Supreme Master Luciphage is proudly exhibited on a 
nearby wall. There are 2 wights here. Swirling eddies of chaotic ether dance 
around a marble shrine to Morgfyre that holds a crystal model of the 
planispheres. A pallid taint wyrm with knife-edged teeth is coiled on the ground
here, blackening the earth beneath him with his corrosive stench. Crying out the

</font><font color="#808000">Centre of the Necropolis.
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">Rubescent lambency emits from amidst crimson petals of the weeping amaranth 
suspended from a magnificent gemwork chandelier.</font><font color="#008080"> Rising up from cracks in the 
floor, the Megalith of Doom towers above everything here, polluting the air with
its foul fumes. The Keeper of the Megalith stands here radiating a tainted 
presence. A painting of Supreme Master Luciphage is proudly exhibited on a 
nearby wall. There are 2 wights here. Swirling eddies of chaotic ether dance 
around a marble shrine to Morgfyre that holds a crystal model of the 
planispheres. A pallid taint wyrm with knife-edged teeth is coiled on the ground
here, blackening the earth beneath him with his corrosive stench. Crying out the
latest news, Rasshid d'Sifal strolls purposefully through the streets.
